# Vantiva Unveils Revolutionary Wi-Fi 7 Condor 5G FWA Home Gateway 
03 Mar 2025 
|
9 min
Barcelona, Spain – March 3, 2025 – **Vantiva (Euronext Paris: VANTI)** , a global technology leader in connectivity, officially launches the Condor 5G Fixed Wireless Access (FWA) home gateway at Mobile World Congress 2025—an advanced, industry-leading platform designed to deliver exceptional indoor 5G connectivity, with performance approaching that of outdoor units. Aimed at tech-forward homes and businesses, the Condor 5G builds on its predecessors, the Cobra 5G and Falcon 5G, elevating in-home wireless experiences with cutting-edge innovations and a sustainable design.
## Cutting-Edge Performance Meets Sleek Innovation
The growth of FWA deployments often saturates cellular networks, particularly on lower bands. Vantiva’s engineers introduced several key innovations to the Condor 5G to address spectrum efficiency challenges while enhancing performance:
  * Near-Window Form Factor: Optimized to boost 5G performance when placed near windows. Its sleek, unobtrusive design integrates seamlessly into any home environment while facilitating ideal placement.
  * Indoor5G™ 180° Antenna System: Features up to 8 antennas, including patented boosters for mid-band connectivity (2.5–4.2 GHz), delivering up to 11 dBi gain with high efficiency. Developed by Vantiva’s antenna team, the system enhances 5G spectrum utilization, expands base station coverage, and prevents network congestion by supporting more connected users.
  * RuralBoost™ Technology: Provides increased receive sensitivity on low bands when the network requires it, reducing the strain on this critical part of the spectrum.
  * 8Rx Capability: Equipped with 8 receive antennas, the Condor 5G ensures extended coverage and high reliability, particularly in challenging environments with physical barriers or long distances. By leveraging experience from the Cobra 5G Xtream, the world’s first 8Rx 5G indoor CPE. The Condor 5G offers full 8Rx support on n38, n41, n77, and n78 bandwidths.


> “We are excited to see our Qualcomm Dragonwing™ FWA Gen 3 platform integrated to power Vantiva’s Condor 5G offering and Indoor5G™ 180° antenna technology,” said Gautam Sheoran, Vice President and General Manager, Wireless Broadband & Communications at Qualcomm Technologies, Inc. “We look forward to seeing operators dramatically expand their FWA service coverage while connecting more homes with high-performance 5G broadband service.”
## Advanced Features for Next-Level Connectivity
The Condor 5G is built with advanced components to ensure durability and future readiness for both consumers and operators over the next five years. Key features include:
  * 3GPP Release 17 Modem Technology: Fully interoperable with Tier-1 operators’ 5G networks, including support for advanced carrier aggregation in NSA and SA (2 CC in the uplink and up to 4x nR-CC in the downlink).
  * Dual-Band Wi-Fi 7 (BE7200): A 4×4 configuration delivers seamless multi-device connectivity with powerful antennas on both 2.4 GHz and 5 GHz channels, ensuring maximum Wi-Fi coverage throughout the home.
  * NaviGate Companion™ App: Offers users an intuitive smartphone application for simple self-installation, management, and control of their FWA setup


## Delivering Value to Operators
The Condor 5G integrates Vantiva’s [Homeware™, an OpenWRT middleware solution](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/vantiva-homeware/) utilized by Tier-1 operators globally. Its container-based architecture supports a broad range of third-party applications, enabling operators to provide FWA subscribers access to the same value-added services typically reserved for fiber, copper, or cable customers.  
Additional operator benefits include support for USP TR-369/TR-181 data models extended to cellular data, seamless remote management, and scalability via firmware-over-the-air (FOTA) updates—all pre-integrated with Vantiva’s ECO-Manage/Control platform.
## Sustainable Design
Vantiva prioritized sustainability in the Condor 5G, incorporating features like halogen-free PCBs, optional use of recycled resins, and a fanless passive cooling solution to reduce environmental impact. A data-driven power consumption optimization feature further ensures efficient energy use.  
“With the Condor 5G, Vantiva is setting a new standard for [FWA home gateways](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/broadening-access-to-better-5g-broadband/),” said Ashwani Saigal, SVP Global Product Management at Vantiva. “By combining cutting-edge technology with sustainable design, we enable telecom operators to deliver unparalleled connectivity experiences to their customers while promoting a greener future.”
## Availability
The Condor 5G will be available beginning March 2025 for telecom providers and enterprise partners.
## About Vantiva
**Pushing the Edge**  
Vantiva (Euronext Paris: VANTI) is a global technology leader in the Customer Premises Equipment (CPE) market. For over 130 years, Vantiva (formerly known as Technicolor) has delivered solutions that connect what matters most. Today, the company continues to redefine connectivity with industry-leading broadband, video, and IoT-driven smart systems that elevate how people live, work, and connect globally.  
Vantiva combines a customer-focused approach with decades of software development, electronics hardware design, and supply chain expertise to deliver high-quality solutions at scale. This proficiency has positioned Vantiva as a trusted provider to leading network service providers, enterprise customers, and consumers around the world.  
A strong commitment to sustainability and responsible business practices has earned Vantiva multiple Gold and Platinum Medals from EcoVadis for environmental and social performance. These awards place the company among the top 2% of organizations in its category evaluated globally.  
With its headquarters in Paris and major offices in Australia, Brazil, China, India, South Korea, the United Kingdom, and the United States, the company serves a diverse global customer base. The acquisition of CommScope’s Home Networks business in January 2024 further bolstered the company and its ongoing commitment to innovation.  
For more information, please visit [vantiva.com](http://vantiva.com) and follow Vantiva on [LinkedIn](https://www.linkedin.com/company/vantiva/) and [X (Twitter).](https://twitter.com/vantiva)

## Our Values
Our values bring us together and make us stronger. They guide how we work, connect, and grow—as a team and with our customers.  
By keeping our customers at the center, simplifying with purpose, taking ownership of our actions, and lifting each other up, we embody what it means to be a United Vantiva.
### Customers at the Center
We walk every step of the journey with our customers, driven by a passion to make a difference. By listening intently, caring deeply, and crafting meaningful solutions, we go beyond being service providers to become trusted partners. We share in our customers’ challenges, celebrate their victories, and continuously strive to earn and keep their trust.
### Innovate and Simplify: Create with Purpose
We deliver true innovation that makes things work better for everyone by rethinking what’s complicated and turning it into something practical and impactful. Our goal is to make both our actions and innovative solutions more intuitive, accessible, and meaningful to all.
### Responsibility: Own It
We lead by example, taking full ownership of our commitments, our work, and our impact on the world. Every decision we make reflects our dedication to integrity, ethical standards, and the communities we serve. We always act with intention and accountability.
### Winning Together: Build with Trust and Teamwork
Collaboration is the heartbeat of our success. We win by bringing diverse perspectives together, supporting each other, and achieving shared goals. Trust is our cornerstone, empowering every team member to show up, speak up, and lift each other up.
## Our Commitments to Business Performance
### **The Tangible Outcome of our Actions**
#### **OnTime**
We deliver reliable, timely solutions that keep our stakeholders ahead in a fast-moving market.
#### **OnQuality**
We focus on superior craftsmanship and precision to meet the highest standards for our stakeholders.
#### **OnMargin**
We build sustainable value to support continuous innovation and evolving stakeholder needs.
#### The Vantiva Story
With 130 years of innovation, Vantiva is ready for the future
  * 1892-1893 
**1892** : General Electric Company is formed through the merger of Thomson-Houston Electric Company and Edison General Electric.
**1893** : Compagnie Française Thomson-Houston (CFTH) is established in Paris.
  * 1966-1988 
**1966** : CFTH merges with Hotchkiss-Brandt to form Thomson-Houston-Hotchkiss-Brandt (later renamed Thomson-Brandt).
**1968** : Thomson-Brandt’s electronics business merges with Compagnie Générale de Télégraphie Sans Fil (CSF) to create Thomson-CSF.
**1982** : Thomson-Brandt and Thomson-CSF are nationalized and merged to form Thomson SA.
**1988** : General Electric sells its consumer electronics division to Thomson to form Thomson Consumer Electronics.
  * 1995-2010 
**1995** : The French government splits Thomson Multimedia and Thomson-CSF, leading to privatization in 1999.
**2000** : Thomson-CSF becomes Thales; Thomson Multimedia buys Technicolor and expands into broadcast management.
**2005** : Major acquisitions, including Cirpack and Inventel; Part of the business is sold to TCL.
**2010** : The Infinity camcorder is discontinued; The Color Picture Tube manufacturing business is sold to Videocon.
  * 2015-2021 
**2015** : Technicolor acquired The Mill and the Set-Top Box and Cable Modem business, formerly known as Scientific Atlanta from Cisco.
**2017** : Technicolor acquires the Set-Top Box divisions from LG and Pioneer
**2018** : Sale of Patent Licensing business to InterDigital.
**2021** : Technicolor Creative Studios is launched; Technicolor Post-Production business is sold to Streamland Media.
  * 2022-2024 
**2022** : Technicolor announces the launch of two separately listed companies: Technicolor Creative Studios and Vantiva.
**2024** : Vantiva acquires CommScope’s Home Networks division, which traces its history back to 1950 with the formation of Jerrold Electronics, a pioneer in CATV, acquired by General Instrument (GI) in 1967:
– 2000: Motorola acquires GI
– 2013: Motorola’s Mobility Home business becomes part of ARRIS Inc.
– 2016: ARRIS Inc. Purchases Pace PLC
– 2017: CommScope acquires ARRIS

## Be Yourself  
**Be Vantiva**
Innovation is at the core of who we are. Our diverse team drives groundbreaking solutions that shape tomorrow. We are bold thinkers, creators, and problem-solvers, united by the belief that authenticity fuels greatness. 
Here, your unique perspective pushes the boundaries of what’s possible, powering our collective success. Ready to shape the future with us? Explore our opportunities and help write the next chapter of our legacy.
## Our Values
####  Responsibility: Own It
We own our commitments, act with integrity, and consider our impact.

We connect with our customers, evolve with their needs, and create lasting impact. 
#### Innovate and Simplify: Create with Purpose
We turn complexity into practical and impactful solutions. 
#### Winning Together: Build with Trust and Teamwork
We succeed through trust, collaboration, and mutual support.

4,000+ employees, 50 nationalities, 20 countries.
  * Inclusive Culture 
Safe, respectful, and equitable environment.
  * People-First Approach 
Empowering every individual to be their authentic self.

## We cultivate sustainability practices
**We are committed to reducing our environmental impact through prioritizing renewable sources, advancing energy-saving technologies, and practicing circularity.**
Creating a sustainable future for our planet is a global effort, and we’re dedicated to executing sustainable actions that have an impact and influence within our industry and beyond. Every step we take aims to preserve our planet for future generations, ensuring our footprint is smaller and smarter than yesterday.
  * [ Our commitment to a greener industry  ](https://www.vantiva.com/esg/sustainability/)
  * [ Climate change  ](https://www.vantiva.com/esg/climate-change/)
  * [ Circular economy  ](https://www.vantiva.com/esg/circular-economy/)


## We empower our people and communities
**We believe in the power of diversity and inclusion.**
Our company is made up of nearly 5,000 individuals representing over 33 nationalities in 20 countries across the globe. To be a part of Vantiva is to be seen, respected, and celebrated as the unique individual you are, a level of nurturing and acknowledgment that sends ripples of equity and inclusion beyond our walls and into our communities.
  * [ Human rights  ](https://www.vantiva.com/esg/human-rights/)

## Nous sommes à vos côtés
**Vantiva redéfinit la manière dont les gens se connectent. En tant que leader technologique mondial, nous créons des produits innovants qui relient en toute fluidité les individus aux contenus et services qui enrichissent leur vie — que ce soit à la maison, au travail ou dans des environnements intelligents à travers le monde.**
Forts de 25 ans d’expérience auprès des acteurs leaders des télécoms, du logiciel et et du jeu, et avec des racines dans l’industrie du divertissement qui remontent à plus d’un siècle, nous apportons une expertise inégalée dans la fabrication de précision, la logistique et l’optimisation de la chaîne d’approvisionnement. Nos solutions sont conçues pour dépasser les attentes et favoriser la réussite de nos clients en Amérique, en Asie-Pacifique, en Europe, au Moyen-Orient et en Afrique.
La durabilité est au cœur de tout ce que nous faisons. De la conception des produits à la logistique mondiale, nous nous engageons à adopter des pratiques respectueuses de l’environnement et des opérations responsables, veillant à ce que notre impact s’étende au-delà du monde de notre activité — au bénéfice de nos partenaires et de la planète.
#### Comment pouvons-  
nous vous aider ?
Cliquez sur le bouton qui vous correspond, on s’occupe du reste !

## Manifeste de la marque Vantiva
Nous connectons ce qui compte pour que vous puissiez vous connecter à ce qui importe.
## Nos équipes façonnent le futur
Notre ambition, notre diversité et notre engagement ouvrent des perspectives infinies, stimulent l’innovation et créent de nouvelles opportunités dans le monde entier. Rejoignez-nous et faites partie d’une équipe où votre potentiel ne connaît pas de limites et où, ensemble, nous créons l’avenir.
[ Voir les offres d'emploi  ](https://www.vantiva.com/fr/career/)
#### Nos engagements
L’engagement de Vantiva en matière de responsabilité sociale des entreprises, qui remonte à plus de 100 ans, se concentre sur les questions sociétales, environnementales et économiques. Les principaux domaines sont les droits de l’homme, la diversité, le changement climatique, l’éco-conception et les chaînes d’approvisionnement durables.
  * Engagement RSE 
Nous mettons l’accent sur les droits de l’homme, la diversité, l’action climatique et la durabilité.
  * Diversité mondiale 
Plus de 4 000 employés, 50 nationalités, 20 pays.
  * Culture inclusive 
Un environnement sûr, respectueux et équitable.
  * Une approche centrée sur les personnes 
Donner à chacun les moyens de grandir.

## Shaping the future  
**of the industry responsibility**
As a forward-looking connected home leader, Vantiva is committed to the highest stand, driving ecological initiatives that ensure a cleaner future for generations to come. In that purpose, we actively collaborate with three benchmark organizations, enabling us to grow while significantly reducing our environmental impact.
  * SCIENCE BASED TARGETS 
Vantiva is dedicated to following the Science Based Targets initiative’s (SBTi) Net-Zero Standard and the Business Ambition for 1.5°C, aiming to lower our business emissions.
  * ECOVADIS PLATINUM STATUS 
EcoVadis placed Vantiva in the top 1% of its industry, awarding us the highest ratings in Environment, Labor & Human Rights, Ethics, and Sustainable Procurement.
  * RESPONSIBLE BUSINESS ALLIANCE 
We drive environmental, social, and governance through our supply chain with a strong focus on CO2 reduction.

#  Smart Spaces
## What are **Smart Spaces**? 
**Step into the future with Smart Spaces, where hyperconnected technology transforms commercial environments into adaptive and intelligent settings for improved operations and new revenue sources.**
These spaces enhance comfort and boost productivity by seamlessly integrating digital solutions into the physical world, creating an environment that is always in tune with your commercial needs.
Automate facility management and leverage data analysis to improve energy efficiency and support predictive maintenance, promoting sustainability and remote work. Enhance user experience through connectivity and personalized interactions, driving efficiency and a superior consumer experience.
Automation and Control 
Data Collection and Analysis 
Sustainability 
Enhanced Connectivity and Integration 
Data-driven Insights 
Personalization 
Enhanced User Experience

# HomeSight
## Connected care – made for tv
[ Contact Us  ](https://www.vantiva.com/contact/)
##  ![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/09/homesight_vantiva_logo.png)Overview
The HomeSight® solution connects older adults with caregivers, care professionals, family and friends through the technology they find most familiar — the TV — creating simple, secure access to a network of trusted people who can contribute to their well-being and help them live independently for longer.
## A whole new perspective on connected care for care providers
The HomeSight system delivers services that can help care providers elevate health and wellness for individuals and their support networks.
## Introducing the new Wellness Module
Secure collection of data from supported 3rd party wireless-connected health devices. The data is made available to authorized caregivers via the HomeSight web portal.
### Home care provider solutions
The HomeSight system enables domiciliary care providers to deliver blended care, complementing in-person care with remote care options to elevate health and wellness, using technology familiar to older adults, the TV.
[ Find out more ](https://www.vantiva.com/homesight/home-care/)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/09/wheelchair.png)
### Residential care and assisted living solutions
Raise the level of care and improve efficiency in residential care homes and assisted living facilities.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/10/family_homesight.png)
## Better home care,  
**delivered more efficiently**
  * CONNECT 
Securely connect older adults, family & friends and caregivers, through the TV — delivering instant access to a network of trusted people that can contribute to better health, reduce isolation, and encourage social engagement for aging adults.
  * ENGAGE 
On-screen health and wellness reminders encourage medical and wellness regime adherence while access to virtual communities helps to keep minds active, bodies healthy and social calendars full.
  * MONITOR 
Virtual lifestyle and wellness monitoring using environmental sensors and paired medical devices deliver actionable data that you can use to improve and customize care for those you serve.

## Protecting sensitive client data
The HomeSight platform complies with the physical, network, and process security measures required by the USA Health Insurance Portability and Accountability Act (HIPAA) to ensure sensitive patient data is protected.

#  Smart Storage  
for self storage operators
## Overview
Our innovative smart self storage platform is highly customizable, future-proof, and integrates seamlessly with third-party technologies.
The platform focuses on creating smart ecosystems for self-storage property portfolios, providing operational efficiencies, new revenue streams, and improved overall functionality.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/09/wheel_square.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/09/Vantiva-smart-spaces-smart-storage-benefits-scaled.jpeg)
  * Operational Efficiency
  * New Revenue Opportunities
  * Safety & Security
  * Tenant Experience


Drive Operational Efficiency
Smart self storage solutions streamline management processes, automate tasks, and optimize resource utilization, leading to increased operational efficiency and cost savings.
Create New Revenue Opportunities
Provide customers with new services that make units smarter and provides a new level of peace of mind
Enhance Safety & Security
Smart self storage solutions incorporate advanced security features like real-time monitoring, access control, and surveillance, enhancing safety and bolstering overall facility security.
Elevate Tenant Experience
Smart self storage amenities such as smart unit cameras, mobile apps, remote access and personalized controls enhance tenant convenience, engagement, and satisfaction.
![facility](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/09/facil.png)
![connectivity_facility](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/09/facility_wifi.png)
![facility_economu](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/09/facility_eco.png)
![facilities_management](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/09/facility_managelet.png)
![facility_safety](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/09/facility_safety.png)
![smart_unit_facility](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/09/facility_violet.png)
  * ######  Site-wide Connectivity  Show more about Site-wide Connectivity
Enables seamless communication and data exchange across all areas of the storage facility, ensuring efficient operations and connectivity between devices.
  * ######  Energy Management  Show more about Energy Management
Utilizes smart technology to monitor and optimize energy usage within the storage facility, promoting sustainability and cost savings.
  * ######  Facilities Management  Show more about Facilities Management
Collects data and integrates sub-systems to oversee and enhance the site maintenance, cleanliness, and functionality.
  * ######  Safety and Security  Show more about Safety and Security
Implements advanced security measures such as access controls, surveillance systems, and monitoring protocols to safeguard the premises and ensure the site safety.
  * ######  Smart Units  Show more about Smart Units
Integrates temperature and humidity sensors, motion detectors and camera technology within storage units to provide real-time monitoring and remote access control capabilities.

## Peek
## Smart Unit Camera
**Transform your self-storage business, delight your customers, and unlock new revenue opportunities with Vantiva Peek™ and its companion app.**
The one-of-a-kind integrated smart camera has built-in sensors that detect motion, measure temperature and humidity and configurable image capture. It also comes equipped with an easy-to-mount magnetic backing and has a long battery life of up to two years.

## Frequently Asked Question
  * What is Smart Self-Storage? 
Smart Self-Storage integrates connected technologies into storage facilities, enabling remote management, enhanced security, and improved operational efficiency. Vantiva’s Smart Storage solutions provide site-wide connectivity, real-time monitoring, and data-driven insights to optimize your storage operations and tenant experiences.
  * What types of connected devices are used in Smart Storage? 
Vantiva’s Smart Storage solutions utilize a range of connected devices, including smart cameras, access control systems, temperature and humidity sensors, leak detectors, and occupancy sensors. These devices are integrated into a unified platform that allows for easy management and monitoring of your storage facilities.
  * Why should my storage facility invest in Smart Storage technology? 
Investing in Smart Storage technology gives you a competitive edge by improving operational efficiency, enhancing tenant satisfaction, and unlocking new revenue streams. With cloud-based management and connected device integration, you can streamline operations, reduce costs, and offer modern features that attract tech-savvy renters.
  * What is robust site-wide coverage, and why is it essential for self-storage sites? 
Robust site-wide coverage ensures seamless connectivity across your entire facility, allowing connected devices to function reliably in every corner. This is crucial for maintaining security, remote monitoring, and ensuring that all smart devices in your facility work without interruptions, even in challenging environments with steel and concrete structures.
  * How does Smart Storage improve operational efficiency? 
Smart Storage improves operational efficiency by automating routine tasks, providing real-time alerts, and offering remote management capabilities. With Vantiva’s cloud-based storage facility management software, you can monitor multiple sites from a single dashboard, reducing the need for on-site staff and enabling predictive maintenance.
  * Can Smart Storage generate additional revenue for my storage facility? 
Yes, Smart Storage can open up new revenue opportunities by offering premium features such as in-unit monitoring with the Vantiva Peek smart camera. You can also offer remote climate control, 24/7 access, smart locks, and more as add-ons, allowing you to charge higher rates for units equipped with advanced technology.
  * How does Smart Storage enhance tenant satisfaction? 
Smart Storage enhances tenant satisfaction by providing features like remote in-unit monitoring, customized climate control, and easy access through mobile apps. Tenants appreciate the convenience and security of managing their storage units digitally, and they’re willing to pay more for improved peace of mind.
  * How does cloud-based management benefit my storage facility? 
Cloud-based management provides the flexibility to access and control your storage facilities from anywhere, at any time. It simplifies data management, enables real-time monitoring, and ensures that your facility can scale easily as you add more IoT devices or expand to new locations.
  * Is Smart Storage scalable for growing storage portfolios? 
Absolutely. Vantiva’s Smart Storage solutions are designed to be scalable, allowing you to manage dozens or even hundreds of sites from a single interface. As your portfolio grows, you can easily add new connected devices and features without major infrastructure changes.
  * What support does Vantiva offer after implementing Smart Storage? 
Vantiva provides ongoing support, including system monitoring, maintenance, and updates to ensure that your Smart Storage solution remains up-to-date and fully operational. We also offer training for your team and continuous improvements based on emerging technologies.
  * How secure is the Smart Storage system? 
Security is a top priority in Vantiva’s Smart Storage solutions. We offer end-to-end encryption, secure cloud storage, and robust access control measures to protect your facility and tenant data. Our system is designed to ensure that only authorized users have access to sensitive information and controls.

## Executive Leadership Team
Leveraging on their diverse background and expertise, the Executive Leadership Team leads Vantiva’s ambition through engaging all Vantiva Teams across businesses and geographies through a journey of innovation, operational excellence and inclusion.
![tim_picture](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/Tim_pic.png)
Read full bio ![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/themes/vantiva-theme/public/images/svg/Arrow-forward.93bc44.svg)
Tim O'Loughlin
Chief Executive Officer
[×](https://www.vantiva.com/our-governance/)
![tim_picture](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/Tim_pic.png)
[ ![linkedin](https://www.vantiva.com/app/themes/vantiva-theme/public/images/svg/linkedin.8001e5.svg) ](https://www.linkedin.com/in/tim-o-loughlin-14351a79/)
####  Tim O'Loughlin
Chief Executive Officer
Tim O'Loughlin led Vantiva’s Connected Home Customer Unit in the Americas from January to October 2024. With over 20 years of experience in business leadership, Mr. O’Loughlin has worked with various telecommunications equipment providers, including previously owned CommScope companies, Arris and Pace. In his most recent role, O’Loughlin served over four years as EVP and President of the Americas Region at Verifone, a global payment services and hardware provider. His leadership roles throughout his career have granted him commercial ownership in the Americas, allowing him to gain a deep understanding of the region and forge strong relationships with a wide variety of customers. Mr. O’Loughlin is passionate about building and inspiring diverse teams and has a proven track record of driving business growth. He sits on the advisory board for TruRating LTD, holds two degrees from Florida Atlantic University and two technical patents. He is based in Fort Lauderdale, Florida, USA.
![aline_bourcereau](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2025/02/Untitled-design-99.png)
Read full bio ![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/themes/vantiva-theme/public/images/svg/Arrow-forward.93bc44.svg)
Aline Bourcereau
Chief Compliance & Sustainability Officer
[×](https://www.vantiva.com/our-governance/)
![aline_bourcereau](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2025/02/Untitled-design-99.png)
[ ![linkedin](https://www.vantiva.com/app/themes/vantiva-theme/public/images/svg/linkedin.8001e5.svg) ](https://www.linkedin.com/in/aline-bourcereau-9a4309a9/)
####  Aline Bourcereau
Chief Compliance & Sustainability Officer
Aline Bourcereau has served as VANTIVA's Chief Compliance Officer since 2022, overseeing and managing the company's compliance risks. A former French lawyer with expertise in white-collar crime, she has extensive experience identifying and mitigating criminal and regulatory risks within industrial sectors. She began her compliance career at Airbus in 2016, where she held various roles in the Defense and Space division and later at the company’s headquarters in Toulouse, France. Following this, she served as Group Compliance Manager at Keolis. Mrs Bourcereau holds a master's degree in Private Law and Criminal Sciences. She was also an assistant to an investigating judge at the Pôle Financier de Paris, and obtained a certification in Fraud detection in 2017. She is based in Paris, France.
![dan_pic](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/11/Dan-zambrano-NEW.png)

Dan Zambrano
Chief Legal Officer
[×](https://www.vantiva.com/our-governance/)

####  Dan Zambrano
Chief Legal Officer
Mr. Zambrano is the Chief Legal Officer of VANTIVA, responsible for managing the commercial, litigation, and strategic legal affairs of the business. He has extensive experience in the technology and entertainment industries and began his career as a litigator before transitioning to M&A and corporate transactions. He joined Vantiva in 2016, rising to serve as the General Counsel to the Connected Home Division. Prior to Vantiva, he served as a member of the international legal department of Turner Broadcasting, managing the legal affairs of television networks such as CNN, TBS, TNT, and Cartoon Network, with an emphasis on technology transactions. A graduate of the University of Pennsylvania, George Washington University Law School, and Emory University's Goizueta Business School, Mr. Zambrano is based in Atlanta, Georgia.

####  Olga Damiron
Chief People and Talent Officer
Ms. Olga Damiron is Chief People and Talent Officer at VANTIVA. With over 20 years of experience leading international teams, she brings a deep understanding of high-technology manufacturing operations in B2B and B2B2C industries to oversee strategic growth projects, change management and transformation initiatives. Her diverse family background allows her to always remember that people are unique and that engaging teams in the ongoing change journey requires authenticity, passion, and consistency. She is based in Paris, France.

####  Lars Ihlen
Chief Financial Officer
Mr. Lars Ihlen is the Chief Financial Officer for VANTIVA, responsible for finance and real estate. He has 25 years of experience in the telecommunication industry, and served the last 11 years as CFO for the Connected Home Division of Technicolor. Prior to that, Mr. Ihlen held various positions in finance for Alcatel-Lucent and Mikron Infokom. Mr. Lars is born and educated in Norway, and during his carrier he has lived in Paris, Shanghai, Los Angeles and Atlanta. He is based in Atlanta, Georgia.

####  Phil Baldock
Group Chief Operating Officer
Mr. Baldock is the Chief Operating Officer of Vantiva, leading supply chain, operations, IT, quality and global transformation. With over 20 years of industry experience, he brings significant expertise in operations and finance, directing wide-scale initiatives in dynamic environments. Mr. Baldock joined Vantiva in 2021 as SVP, Regional Business Center Americas managing the customer delivery, technical support and business operations functions. His prior experience in the Telecommunications industry included positions as SVP, Chief Information Officer at ARRIS leading a global systems transformation program and SVP, Business Operations at Pace plc operationalizing revenue growth. Mr. Baldock qualified as a Chartered Management Accountant in the UK, holds a bachelor’s degree in accounting from Glasgow Caledonian University and an MBA from the University of Florida. He is based in Atlanta, GA.

####  Navneeth Kannan
Senior Vice President, Diversification Solutions
Mr Kannan leads the Retail and HomeSight businesses. He brings 40 years of experience in computing and telecommunications industry, in both corporate and startup environments, with extensive leadership roles in Software, Systems Engineering, and Product Management. Prior to joining Vantiva, Mr kannan was leading the Diversification effort as part of the CommScope Home Networks and incubated HomeSight from concept to commercial launch. He is passionate about technology and has 20 granted patents. He holds a Bachelor’s degree in Electronics Engineering and a Master’s degree in Computer Science. Mr Kannan is based in Philadelphia, Pennsylvania, United States.

####  David Olival
Chief Information and Security Officer
Mr. David Olival is the Chief Information and Security Officer of Vantiva, responsible for overseeing the company’s information systems and cybersecurity. With over 25 years of industry experience, he brings deep expertise in leading global transformation programs, M&A activities, business carve-outs, and IT governance. He previously served as CIO for the Connected Home, Patents & Licensing, and Corporate Functions divisions of Technicolor. Earlier in his career, he held several IT management roles at Thomson Multimedia and Essilor International. Mr. Olival holds a Master’s degree in Management and Organization of Information Systems. He is based in Paris, France.

####  Frederic Chapelard

#### Board of Directors  

The Board of Directors of Vantiva reflects the diversity of our global markets. Its member are responsible for making sure the interests of all shareholders are taken into account and that Vantiva meets its long term goals. The Board of Directors ensure that the Executive and Management Committees act in the best interests of the company and its shareholders.

####  Tony Werner
Independent Director
Mr. Tony Werner has spent the last 16 years at Comcast Cable, as Chief Technology Officer, then President of the Technology-Product-Experience Division. Mr. Werner is a reference in the world of telecommunications and technology where he is recognized as a leader and innovator. Prior to joining Comcast, he held leadership positions at Liberty Global, Inc., Aurora Networks, Tele-Communications, Inc. (TCI)/AT&T Broadband and Rogers Communications. Mr. Werner was Chairman and Chairman of the Board of Directors of the Society of Cable Telecommunications Engineers (SCTE) and the SCTE Foundation from 2015 to 2017. He was Chairman of the Technical Action Committee (TAC) of CableLabs from 2007 to 2022 and a member of the Board of Directors of Kyrio, the commercial arm of CableLabs. In addition, Mr. Werner has been inducted into the Cable and Broadcast Hall of Fame and the Cable Center Hall of Fame. In 2000, Tony Werner received the NCTA Vanguard Award for Science and Technology. Later in 2016, he received the Technical Emmy Award for Lifetime Achievement.

#### Corporate governance code of reference
Vantiva adheres to the Afep-Medef Corporate Governance Code of December 2022 in the preparation of the Report as defined by article L. 225-37 of the French Commercial Code.

# Broadband solutions
Overview 
## A revolution in **broadband technology**
We are dedicated to enabling premium access experiences throughout every home. With powerful broadband and intelligent Wi-Fi® technologies, we enable Multi-User Gigabit Services across every corner of the home.

OUR VISION 
## Broadband is about  
**more than broadband**
As a global leader in broadband, Vantiva envisions its platforms as more than just Internet access, but as a gateway to a superior user experience—from streaming and remote work to online gaming and beyond.
In collaboration with our partners, we deliver a unique broadband experience, combining AI-powered features, ultra-high speeds, ultra-low latency, user-friendly interfaces, high value-added services, and sustainability.
Technologies 
### Fiber
**The Fastest Speeds in Broadband.**
Vantiva’s versatile fiber solutions allow you to upgrade as your infrastructure evolves, consistently delivering high-speed broadband, exceptional in-home wireless coverage, and an expanding array of home services & applications.
[ Read more ](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/bringing-fiber-home/)

**Rely on the Pioneering Leader in DOCSIS® Technology.**
As the global leader in DOCSIS® 3.0 and 3.1 gateways, Vantiva ensures top-tier, high-performance equipment and propels you forward with cutting-edge 3.1+ and 4.0 technologies for unmatched speeds.

**Take Ultra-Fast Broadband Wherever Your Subscribers Are.**
Leveraging our unparalleled antenna expertise and exclusive proprietary technologies, Vantiva’s 5G Fixed Wireless Access solutions significantly boost coverage, connection stability, and broadband speeds for subscribers in urban, suburban and rural areas.

### Routers
**Turning Homes into Connectivity Hubs.**

### Extenders
**Target Zero Dead Zone.**
Whatever the Wi-Fi® standard, your wireless network performance is only as strong as the living space allows. For faster, unwavering broadband from basement to loft, Vantiva developed a range of extenders embedding the latest mesh solutions, rigorously tested by our engineering teams under the most demanding conditions.

**Software & services**
## Software magic for  
**a superior user experience**
Our gateways do more than provide Internet access—they deliver an extraordinary user experience across all technologies.  
With embedded software stacks supporting diverse services and applications, they also ensure indispensable protection for local networks.
![someone_typing_computer](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/68d882ef74401409c0ef01ed264a57f4.png)
  * HOMEWARE™
  * RDK-B
  * PRPL
  * Professional Services


![homeware_logo](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/c872877b9e7952f9fc105ca526ae1e54.png)
Homeware™ is Vantiva’s software solution for OpenWRT home gateways. An open-source SDK for service providers, Homeware™ provides a standard platform to build, deploy, and support new services more efficiently. We have extended OpenWRT to make it carrier-grade while maintaining the overall architecture – the result is an intuitive software solution that is open, apps-ready, interoperable and secure.
![rdk-b_logo](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/rdkb_logo-300x58.png)
Deployed over 125 million Vantiva devices, RDK-B is an innovative open-source platform that powers next-gen broadband gateways, enabling you to easily manage services with enhanced performance and customization. RDK-B ensures seamless integration and superior Wi-Fi management for an exceptional home internet experience.
![prpl_logo](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/propl_logo-300x107.png)
With its prplOS and Life Cycle Management (LCM) solutions, prpl provides a unified middleware that simplifies deployment, allowing operators to dynamically manage and launch unique services efficiently. prpl’s innovative, flexible, and scalable solutions are designed to deliver superior performance and an exceptional home internet experience.​
Our Managed Software Services empower customers to manage their own CPE software stacks and ensure vendor-agnostic gateway compatibility. ​
​
We enhance consumer experiences by customizing device software, developing new gateway apps and containerizing existing ones. ​
​
With our expertise in CPE software development, testing, and deployment, we deliver streamlined integration and optimal performance.​
[ Learn more  ](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/professional-services/)

It also offers user-friendly local network management options with a wide array of features, including security, parental controls, access rights, and more.

**VALUES**
## What our broadband  
**solutions stand for**
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/09/PURPLE_63.png)
###  Innovation
Collaborating closely with chipset vendors, hardware manufacturers, open-source developers, and trusted third-party app providers, Vantiva invests heavily to stay at the forefront of AI, 5G, cable, antenna design, predictive supply chain, and more.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/09/PURPLE_54.png)
###  Quality products
Vantiva aims to exceed customer expectations. Through cutting-edge product design, our advanced antenna laboratory, and rigorous testing, we deliver superior performance in coverage, speed, infrastructure compatibility, and lifespan, outpacing competing gateways.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/09/PURPLE_68.png)
###  Security
Security is built into our products at every stage. Our products use a super-secure boot loader with two-stage authentication using Vantiva generated keys, that ensures only validated software can be loaded onto the device. Vantiva’s dedicated security organization includes security architects & auditors, crypto experts, and an incident response management team. ISO 27001 certified. ​
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/09/PURPLE_3.png)
###  Sustainability
From design to packaging, our engineers are dedicated to shaping the future of our industry. By eliminating unnecessary components, reducing size and power consumption, focusing on refurbishment, optimizing logic, and using recycled or recyclable materials, we strive to minimize the environmental impact of our devices.

# Bringing fiber home
Vantiva’s diverse platforms support GPON, XGS-PON, and 25GS-PON, empowering you to effortlessly upgrade your gateway fleet as your infrastructure evolves.
  * [OVERVIEW](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/bringing-fiber-home/#overview)
  * [BENEFITS](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/bringing-fiber-home/#benefits)
  * [PRODUCTS](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/bringing-fiber-home/#products)


**OVERVIEW**
## From GPON to 25GS-PON  
**& beyond**
The fiber network offers speeds surpassing all other broadband technologies. GPON technology is now succeeded by the XGS-PON standard, with symmetrical speeds of 10Gbps — and the even more powerful 25GS-PON, reaching a staggering 25Gbps to support the requirements for emerging tech well into the future.
Vantiva’s open-source, secure, scalable fiber solutions consistently deliver unparalleled broadband performance and reliability for optimal home connectivity.
Benefits 
## Interoperability:  
**the freedom to choose**
Our gateways and Optical Network Units overcome the challenges of interoperability thanks to the R&D conducted by Vantiva’s Fiber Interoperability Lab. Our team tests all Customer Premises Equipment (CPE) to ensure they are fully compatible with all types of optical line terminals (OLTs) based on an extensive list of OLT models, firmware and patch versions.
A dedicated team of Vantiva experts performs ongoing tests at our customer labs to make sure every home gateway integrates perfectly into any service network.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/hommetoucheecran.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/banner_text1.png)
## Wi-Fi® like you’ve  
**never experienced**
Wi-Fi performance is crucial for seamless access to content across countless wireless devices. We are leveraging 30 years of unparalleled expertise in antenna design to offer you the best of Wi-Fi 6, 6E, and 7 standards.
Our exclusive Vantiva Wi-Fi XL™ solution delivers a more robust and expansive Wi-Fi mesh network. Our exhaustive testing ensures our network effectively translates the speeds of fiber, providing an exceptional user experience.
[ Learn more about Wi-Fi XL  ](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/wireless-connectivity-redefined/)
## Technology **that lasts**
Vantiva prioritizes reliability and durability in its platform designs. Our solutions support remote management standards such as TR-069, enabling smooth, efficient upgrades, proactive issue resolution, and extended product lifespans.
Committed to sustainability, our platforms are crafted using recycled materials, feature plastic-free packaging, offer refurbishing options, and are optimized for energy- and space- efficiency.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/cartemere-1.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/homme_regarde_telephone.png)
## Open to a multiverse **of experiences**
Leverage the power of RDK, prpl, or Vantiva Homeware™, our open-source-based software, to flawlessly integrate third-party services and applications. Simplify network management, enhance parental controls, customize user experiences, and more.
All software stacks are deployable across our platforms, ensuring faster time-to-market and effortless gateway management.
## Network management **at your fingertips**
Vantiva’s NaviGate Companion™ app enables remote management and monitoring of users’ home networks —from anywhere, anytime — along with the option to access value-added services offered by operators.
As a cloud-based solution, NaviGate Companion makes it possible to derive business intelligence that allows operators to gain insights into subscriber activity and to adapt, customize, and evolve their offerings to meet demands.
[ Learn more ](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/navigate-companion/)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/telphione_broadband1.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/banner_new3.png)
## Protection for a complex **ecosystem of connectivity**
**Our fiber gateways & optical network units are built with an overall software architecture that includes an end-to-end security mechanism by design**, covering everything from bootup, firmware upgrades, and gateway configuration to the installation of applications via lifecycle management.
**Vantiva also holds the ISO 27001 certification** , representing a commitment to long-term security and privacy, allowing us to bypass certain NSP compliance checks, saving significant time, cost, and risk throughout the process.

# Broadening access to better 5G broadband
Vantiva’s 5G Fixed Wireless Access solutions significantly boost coverage, connection stability, and broadband speeds for subscribers in urban, suburban, and rural areas.
  * [OVERVIEW](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/broadening-access-to-better-5g-broadband/#overview)
  * [BENEFITS](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/broadening-access-to-better-5g-broadband/#benefits)
  * [PRODUCTS](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/broadening-access-to-better-5g-broadband/#products)


**OVERVIEW**
## Take ultra-fast broadband wherever your subscribers are
5G Fixed Wireless Access (FWA) not only offers a next-generation broadband experience in regions where fiber or cable rollout is limited — it is the perfect complement to mobile offerings and maximizes ROI on spectrum investments.
Leveraging our unique expertise in Wi-Fi and 4G, and building on millions of gateways produced, our FWA CPE provide high and reliable downlink and uplink speeds, improve 5G signal reception indoors, and enable whole-home Wi-Fi coverage.
Benefits 
## Wireless connectivity,  
**wireline quality**
With powerful chipsets, the latest 3GPP standards, and up to 4x carrier aggregation capabilities, Vantiva 5G gateways deliver blazing-fast internet speeds. Perfect for data-intensive applications way beyond mobile use, they provide a broadband experience that seamlessly supports cloud computing, TV, streaming, and gaming — rivaling the efficiency and efficacy of wireline.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/antenne_vert.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/indoor5G_banner1.png)
[![logo_5G](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/logo_indoor5G.svg)](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/logo_indoor5G.svg)
Exclusive to Vantiva’s gateways, Indoor5G™ technology allows simultaneous testing and operation of multiple antennas, ensuring optimal connectivity at all times. Leveraging advanced performance algorithms and high-gain, high-efficiency antennas, Indoor5G™ boosts throughput quality and service area by up to 40% compared to traditional gateways.
![logo_wan](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/logo_wan.png)
Our premium WANsensing™ technology combines a robust cable/fiber connection with 5G capabilities to ensure intelligent and seamless handovers between networks — minimizing mobile data consumption and guaranteeing uninterrupted connectivity, especially for critical applications requiring continuous service.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/cartesim.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/banner_rural.png)
![logo_ruralboost](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/logo_rural-300x157.png)
In the most remote locations, 5G service can be unstable or virtually inaccessible. RuralBoost™ addresses this by improving gateway throughput in low bands by up to 3.5 times. For your subscribers, this translates to a significant enhancement in downlink performance. For you, it means expanding your quality service area and customer base.
## Installation so simple,  
**it’s embarrassing**
The most challenging aspect for operators is often Customer Premises Equipment installation, which can make or break the customer experience before it even begins. Vantiva eliminates this concern with its NaviGate™ suite of mobile applications, empowering users from installation to LAN management.
  * Self-installation with Navigate 5G™ 
NaviGate 5G™ offers guided tips for optimal 5G installation, Augmented Reality-assisted CPE positioning, optimal 5G tower determination, Wi-Fi/Bluetooth® smartphone pairing, and installation validation with speed confirmation.
[ Learn more ](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/navigate-5g/)
  * Network management with Navigate COMPANION™ 
NaviGate Companion™ offers user-friendly local network management options with a wide array of features, including security, parental controls, access rights, and more.
[ Learn more ](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/navigate-companion/)


![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/phoen.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/banner_text1.png)
## Wi-Fi® like you’ve never experienced
Wi-Fi performance is crucial for seamless access to content across countless wireless devices. Our 5G gateways leverage Wi-Fi 6 and Wi-Fi 7 to deliver a more robust and expansive mesh network. Our exhaustive testing ensures our network covers the widest areas, providing an exceptional user experience.
## Technology that lasts
Vantiva prioritizes reliability and durability in its platform designs. Our solutions support remote management standards such as TR-069, enabling smooth, efficient upgrades, proactive issue resolution, and extended product lifespans.
Committed to sustainability, our platforms are crafted using recycled materials, feature plastic-free packaging, offer refurbishing options, and are optimized for energy- and space- efficiency.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/cartemere-1.png)
![condor_5G](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2025/03/Vantiva-Unveils-Revolutionary-Wi-Fi-7-Condor-5G-FWA-Home-Gateway-.png) ![cobra_product](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/cobra5G.png) ![falcon_product](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/falcon.png)

# Leveled up  
cable technology
As the global leader in DOCSIS® gateways and modems, Vantiva is setting the standard with next-generation devices integrated with the latest Wi-Fi® and world-renowned platforms like RDK-B to deliver cutting-edge cable solutions.
  * [OVERVIEW](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/leveled-up-cable-technology/#overview)
  * [BENEFITS](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/leveled-up-cable-technology/#benefits)
  * [PRODUCTS](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/leveled-up-cable-technology/#products)


**OVERVIEW**
## Connectivity built  
**for future innovation**
DOCSIS® cable technology has been, and continues to be, a cornerstone of broadband connectivity. Vantiva maintains an edge on the competition, pioneering incredible advancements in DOCSIS with groundbreaking offerings in DOCSIS 3.1+ and 4.0 technologies.
The latest DOCSIS devices from Vantiva deliver remarkably high bandwidth, reliability, and security, with little latency or lag for a truly exceptional customer experience.
BENEFITS 
## Optimized performance **at top speed**
Vantiva’s latest DOCSIS modems and gateways offer lightning-fast multi-gig download speeds reaching over 10Gbps with the latest standard, enabling faster downloads, uninterrupted video calling, gaming, and 4K streaming, and support for emerging applications and valued-added services to elevate your offerings and increase ROI.
Carefully designed devices promise top-tier performance, regardless of configuration, so you can achieve more — whether it’s with one box or two.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/gaming.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/banner_secure.png)
## Secure by design,  
**managed by command**
Today’s homes and businesses are powered by technology more than ever before, creating a new level of reliance on secure connectivity to protect customers and data at all costs. Our DOCSIS solutions are built with end-to-end security mechanisms to deliver robust security that can be fully managed from anywhere.
This means you can always ensure that your devices are covered from bootup and firmware configurations to upgrades and app installations.
## Wi-Fi like you’ve  
**never experienced**
Wi-Fi performance is crucial for seamless access to content across countless wireless devices.
Our DOCSIS solutions leverage 30 years of unparalleled expertise in antenna design to offer you the best of Wi-Fi 6, 6E, and 7 standards — backed by exhaustive testing at our labs to ensure network coverage that is unmatched.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/occulus.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/assemblage.png)
## Open to a multiverse of experiences
Leverage the power of RDK, prpl, or Vantiva Homeware™, our open-source-based software, to flawlessly integrate third-party services and applications. Simplify network management, enhance parental controls, customize user experiences, and more.
All software stacks are deployable across our platforms, ensuring faster time-to-market and effortless gateway management.
## Network management at your fingertips
Vantiva’s NaviGate Companion™ app enables remote management and monitoring of users’ home networks —from anywhere, anytime — along with the option to access value-added services offered by operators.
As a cloud-based solution, NaviGate Companion makes it possible to derive business intelligence that allows operators to gain insights into subscriber activity and to adapt, customize, and evolve their offerings to meet demands.

# Best in-home **connectivity**
When it comes to connectivity, despite delivering best-in-class broadband to homes and businesses, ultimately, it’s the router that will make or break the user experience.
  * [OVERVIEW](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/best-in-home-connectivity/#overview)
  * [BENEFITS](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/best-in-home-connectivity/#benefits)
  * [PRODUCTS](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/best-in-home-connectivity/#products)


**OVERVIEW**
## Routers that deliver **beyond Wi-Fi®**
From GPON to XGS-PON, DOCSIS 3.1 to 4.0, and 4G/LTE to 5G, major broadband technologies are undergoing significant upgrades, providing unprecedented connection speeds and enabling new use cases.
To extend this experience into homes and businesses, Vantiva designs routers that meet the demands of higher speeds, more connected devices, advancing Wi-Fi® standards, one-click mesh integration and management, and enhanced network security.
BENEFITS 
## Superior connectivity **across technologies**
Ideal for two-box installations, our routers support a range of connection speeds offered by broadband technologies, from 4G and 5G mobile networks to the symmetrical 25Gbps of 25G-PON fiber. They provide multiple wired, wireless, and voice interfaces to meet the diverse needs of homes and businesses.
This ensures a consistent user experience for your subscribers across different networks while limiting development and deployment costs.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/building.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/11/website-hero-banner-584-32.png)
## Professional Wi-Fi® performance
Leveraging our strong relationships with component suppliers, chipset partners, and customers, we design antenna systems that provide best-in-class wireless access with Wi-Fi 6, 6E, and 7.
Our exclusive Vantiva Wi-Fi XL™ solution integrates third-party technologies to simplify device pairing and network management beyond Wi-Fi EasyMesh™.
## Futureproof **technology**
At Vantiva, we focus on creating reliable and durable platform designs. Our routers integrate remote management standards like TR-069, facilitating seamless upgrades, proactive troubleshooting, and extended product lifespans.
And with a host of emerging technologies, applications, and services hitting the market every day, you can trust Vantiva to provide the tools to support you — today, tomorrow, and for what lies ahead.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/lookat.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/Picture1.png)
## Creating a smart environment
Powerful middleware like RDK, prpl, or Vantiva Homeware™, our open-source-based software, enables seamless integration of third-party services and applications. Simplify network management, improve parental controls, personalize user experiences, and more.
## Network management  
**at your fingertips**
Vantiva’s NaviGate Companion™ app enables remote management and monitoring of users’ home networks — from anywhere, anytime — along with the option to access value-added services offered by operators.
As a cloud-based solution, NaviGate Companion makes it possible to derive business intelligence that allows operators to gain insights into subscriber activity and to adapt, customize, and evolve their offerings to meet demands.
[ Learn more ](https://www.vantiva.com/)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/telphione_broadband1.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/banner_new3.png)
## Ensuring secure connectivity  
**across the network**
**Being the entryway to the in-home ecosystem, our routers are designed with a holistic software architecture that incorporates end-to-end security measures**. This includes everything from initial bootup and firmware updates to router configuration and application installation, managed through lifecycle management.
**With our ISO 27001 certification, Vantiva demonstrates a steadfast commitment to security and privacy.** This accreditation helps us streamline certain NSP compliance checks, saving considerable time, reducing costs, and mitigating risks throughout the process.
## Sustainability  
**redefined**
Vantiva’s routers are crafted with sustainability in mind:
  * Made with PCR ABS recycled plastic to reduce waste and carbon footprint.
  * Optimized in size and parts to reduce material, improve logistics and storage.
  * Designed for easy disassembly, enabling quick refurbishment and redeployment to new customers without extra manufacturing.
  * Packaged entirely in recycled carton, plastic-free, with optimized size and parts to minimize waste.

**Extenders**
#  Target zero   
**dead zone**
Your wireless network performance is only as strong as the living space allows. Vantiva’s range of extenders offer seamless connectivity throughout the home via state-of-the-art wireless technology.
  * [OVERVIEW](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/target-zero-dead-zone/#overview)
  * [BENEFITS](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/target-zero-dead-zone/#benefits)
  * [PRODUCTS](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/target-zero-dead-zone/#products)


**OVERVIEW**
## Extend more  
**than a mesh network**
Wi-Fi® extenders are crucial for improving coverage and performance in large areas, multi-floor buildings and environments with multiple devices or weak signal zones. Providing extenders ensures optimal compatibility and performance within the network, enhances customer satisfaction, and facilitates better technical support and troubleshooting.
Benefits 
## Multi-gigabit speeds  
**throughout the home**
Saying that Vantiva extenders merely extend the signal range in the home is an understatement. Our extenders offer state-of-the-art Wi-Fi, leveraging 30 years of expertise and strong partnerships with component suppliers, chipset partners, and customers. Whether it’s the proven Wi-Fi 6 and 6E or the revolutionary Wi-Fi 7, we deploy treasures of engineering and conduct rigorous real-life testing to extend and enhance wireless networks, regardless of your subscribers’ home configuration.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/street.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/girl_phone.png)
## Easy pairing & seamless roaming
Equipped with the Wi-Fi EasyMesh™ standard and high-speed Ethernet ports, our extenders seamlessly integrate into existing networks to enhance their performance.
Beyond seamless roaming, our exclusive Vantiva Wi-Fi XL™ solution incorporates third-party technologies to simplify device pairing and mesh network management.
## Device management,  
**simplified**
Our extenders make network management a breeze with a user-friendly interface accessible both locally and remotely. Easily manage networks through a simple web portal and enjoy seamless remote access for diagnostics. Automated setup and comprehensive management tools ensure everything runs smoothly, while features like zero-touch autoprovisioning make it easy for everyone to use.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/femme_speaking.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/Picture1.png)
## The strongest link  
**in the network**
Like all Vantiva products, our extenders feature an end-to-end security architecture, ensuring protection from bootup to firmware upgrades, configuration, and application installation via lifecycle management.
Vantiva’s ISO 27001 certification underscores our commitment to long-term security and privacy, allowing us to bypass certain NSP compliance checks, saving significant time, cost, and risk.
## Beyond Wi-Fi®:  
**a world of services**
Our extenders are more than just silent network devices. With an open-source software stack, they can become the smart core of your network, allowing you to embed third-party applications for network management, parental control, and much more.
All software stacks are deployable across our platforms, ensuring faster time-to-market and effortless device management.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/child-on-phone.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/assemblage.png)
## Sustainability redefined
**Vantiva’s extenders are crafted with sustainability in mind:**
  * Made with PCR ABS recycled plastic to reduce waste and carbon footprint.
  * Optimized in size and parts to reduce material, improve logistics and storage.
  * Designed for easy disassembly, enabling quick refurbishment and redeployment to new customers without extra manufacturing.
  * Packaged entirely in recycled carton, plastic-free, with optimized size and parts to minimize waste.

**Wi-Fi XL**
# Wireless connectivity redefined
Vantiva Wi-Fi XL is our comprehensive solution designed to optimize home connectivity through state-of-the-art hardware and intelligent software integration to ensure a first-class mesh Wi-Fi® experience. 
  * [OVERVIEW](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/wireless-connectivity-redefined/#overview)
  * [BENEFITS](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/broadband/wireless-connectivity-redefined/#benefits)


## Wi-Fi that fits  
**into any environment**
Wi-Fi XL allows Network Service Providers (NSPs) to deliver a consistent, high-quality wireless experience to their customers, regardless of chipset or operating system, such as RDK, Homeware/OpenWRT, and Prpl, ensuring seamless operation across various technological environments.
Developed through our extensive antenna hardware expertise and close collaboration with leading companies in the mesh industry, Wi-Fi XL is transforming the standards of home Wi-Fi, offering NSPs an exceptional tool to meet the growing demand for uninterrupted in-home connectivity.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/wifi_xl_logo.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/antenna.png)
## Mastery in antenna design
Our antenna design expertise is crucial to the success of Wi-Fi XL and the overall performance of a Wi-Fi device. Facing challenges such as limited space, managing thermal control, and ensuring radiation diversity, our engineers work tirelessly through the design process utilizing simulation, prototyping, lab assessments, field testing, and data analysis to ensure our devices achieve optimal Wi-Fi performance.
The Vantiva Antenna Lab executes this all in-house, investing heavily in testing sites, tools, and technologies to produce products with market-leading performance while also meeting customers’ cost and network demands to deliver a superior consumer experience throughout the home.
## Seamless mesh integration  
**for optimized performance**
Vantiva pre-integrates some of the most innovative 3rd party Mesh solutions to work seamlessly on our latest Customer Premises Equipment (CPE) platforms. As a trusted reference design for these companies, Vantiva CPE pre-integrated with these solutions provide NSPs with a reliable source for deploying innovative Mesh software, ensuring they stay ahead of the curve on the latest developments and innovations compared to competitors’ solutions.
The synergy between Vantiva’s robust hardware and 3rd party advanced software guarantees optimized performance and enhanced interoperability with any connected device. This means lower support costs and calls and increased customer satisfaction.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/wifi_7.png)
## Advanced wi-fi CPE with universal compatibility
Our latest, advanced Wi-Fi 7 CPE, including home gateways, routers, and extenders, provide high-quality, whole-home wireless coverage, eliminating dead zones and delivering multi-gigabit speeds.
Wi-Fi 7 offers the most significant advancements yet for Wi-Fi connectivity, delivering unprecedented speeds and reliability with higher bandwidth, lower latency, and the power to meet the needs of future emerging technologies. And with universal compatibility with chipsets and operating systems, NSPs have freedom and flexibility in hardware and software choices, streamlining deployments and enabling them to provide a consistent customer experience across various equipment combinations.
## Sophisticated  
**Wi-Fi management**
Homes today have more connected devices than ever, making the right management tools essential to NSPs and users alike. With mobile app integration, NSPs can gain valuable data analytics and insights into network performance and consumer behaviors, facilitating optimized service delivery. For customers, Wi-Fi management solutions deliver personalized services that include easy installation, tools for daily use, and simple management of connected devices.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/telphione_broadband1.png)
## How innovative work at Vantiva’s  
**antenna lab improved Wi-Fi coverage**
The strength of your Wi-Fi network often defines customer satisfaction: poor signal strength, buffering issues, dead zones, and the need for extenders can not only frustrate users but also put a strain on your customer support and risk client retention.
Vantiva is at the forefront of resolving these challenges. Our commitment to excellence is showcased through our Antenna Lab, where we engineer world-class Wi-Fi solutions that challenge industry standards.

**Software**
# Navigate Companion™
The NaviGate Companion™ mobile app, available for Android & iOS devices, empowers users to effortlessly and seamlessly configure, monitor, and manage their home gateways in real-time.
**OVERVIEW**
## A network control center **made for mobile devices**
A holistic broadband experience that extends beyond a stable internet connection is now essential. This includes connecting multiple devices, sharing the network with household members or guests, implementing parental controls and timeout rules, addressing security concerns, and conducting performance tests. These use cases collectively form part of a network service provider’s home network offering. NaviGate Companion, a new gateway companion app within Vantiva’s NaviGate software suite, enables remote management and monitoring of users’ home networks, along with access to value-added services offered by operators.
**BENEFITS**
## Navigate Companion™  
**in 5 features**
  * QR-based easy onboarding
  * Easy setup of Wi-Fi guest network
  * Monitoring of all connected devices
  * Ability to define Custom internet access rules
  * Advanced settings for security & more


![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/world.png)
## Cloud-based solution and business intelligence
A cloud-based solution with resident data enables the extraction of valuable business intelligence, allowing operators to gain insights into subscribers’ usage patterns and adjust, customize, and evolve their offerings accordingly. The NaviGate Companion app, being cloud-based, provides users with real-time access from anywhere, facilitating effective monitoring and management of home networks from any location.
## Designed  
**with end user in mind**
The NaviGate Companion app features a user-friendly, personalized interface, ensuring that end users can effortlessly navigate and perform their intended actions. This excellent user experience fosters long-term engagement, service retention, customer satisfaction, and loyalty.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/3phones.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/touchscreen_security.png)
## Seamless integration for more value than ever
The NaviGate Companion solution is capable of seamless integration with operators’ systems. This allows operators to offer their subscribers the option to access value-added services through the NaviGate Companion app, such as security features, gaming optimization, bandwidth slicing, and more.
## A feature list that puts users in control
End users not only get visibility into connected devices and the ability to define the internet access rules, but they can also control advanced Wi-Fi settings. The key features of the NaviGate Companion app include onboarding, monitoring, parental control/timeouts, speed test, Guest Wi-Fi, Wi-Fi networks, security.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/kid_on_phone.png)

**Software**
# Navigate 5G™
The NaviGate 5G™ mobile app, available for Android & iOS devices, empowers subscribers to self-install their 5G gateways and monitor the quality of their 5G connection — intuitively.
**OVERVIEW**
## Self-setup for  
**5G gateways**
5G technology is changing the face of connectivity, delivering unprecedented flexibility with speeds rivaling other technologies. Gateway placement is a critical part of achieving the most effective 5G signal for high speeds and performance throughout the home. Vantiva’s NaviGate 5G™ mobile app is purposefully designed to assist and support end users with efficient, user-friendly self-setup and management of their 5G Fixed Wireless Access (FWA) gateways.
**BENEFITS**
## Navigate 5G™ in 5 features
  * Closest 5G base station geolocation
  * AR-assisted gateway positioning
  * Guide & Tips to install the gateway
  * QR-based Wi-Fi/smartphone pairing
  * Validate the installation and confirm the 5G FWA speed achieved


![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/homme_ouvrier.png)
## 5G gateway setup made cost-efficient
Typical technician gateway installations and setups often require multiple employees for home visits, incurring significant operational and logistics costs and necessitating customer relations management. NaviGate 5G™ offers a self-service solution that allows end users to independently set up their 5G gateways, eliminating the need for home visits. This reduces substantial costs associated with operations, logistics, and client management.
## Designed for new applications
Homeware is an SDK for service providers to develop unique and fully customized applications on their gateways. This enables operators to generate new services and improve average revenue per user (ARPU) or optimize existing services and reduce total cost of ownership (TCO). Third-party developers can easily code compatible apps or choose from a catalog of pre-integrated innovative apps from Vantiva’s HERO Partner Program. One example is Homeware’s Life Cycle Management application, which improves broadband service availability by decoupling application upgrades and maintenance from the gateway core software.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/multi_phone.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/touroperateur.png)
## Beneficial to operators
Vantiva’s NaviGate 5G™ solution provides several key benefits to operators:
  * API Integration: Leverages the operator system via API to access the 5G tower list, ensuring accurate and up-to-date information.
  * Gateway Communication: Communicates with the gateway through Wi-Fi or Bluetooth for precise signal and speed testing.
  * **Serverless Architecture:** Minimizes operational efforts and maintenance due to its serverless design.
  * **Flexible Deployment:** Can be launched from an existing app at the operator’s discretion, offering seamless integration and enhanced user experience.


## Satisfaction and loyalty
NaviGate 5G™ enables subscribers to independently manage their 5G setup and monitor signal quality. Features like signal strength and speed testing allow users to validate their 5G connection, enhancing customer engagement, loyalty, and satisfaction. This self-service offering ensures subscribers can easily optimize their 5G experience, contributing to higher levels of user appreciation and usage.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/woman_typing.png)

  6. | 
  7. RDK-B


# RDK-B supporting  
broadband, video, and IOT
OVERVIEW
## The open-source software platform
The RDK-B (Reference Design Kit for Broadband) is an open-source software platform used to power next-generation gateways. modems, and routers across PON, DOCSIS, 5G, and Ethernet access networks. Part of the RDK platform, RDK-B is a powerful tool for global broadband — unifying a common technical method to ensure consistency between chipset suppliers and OEMs across a range of applications.
As a platform, RDK-B is used across home-networking interfaces, device management, diagnostics, and IoT interfaces, such as Bluetooth®, Thread, and Zigbee®. Every Vantiva DOCSIS home gateway is equipped with RDK-B as the default software stack.
## What can RDK-B **do for you?**
RDK-B is an open platform used by hundreds of companies and thousands of collaborators. This allows these companies to adopt an industry-leading standard of technology without the burden of major development costs and ongoing maintenance. It is an open, flexible platform, allowing operators to enhance their offerings with value-added apps and services, including parental controls, internet attack protection, and wireless mesh technologies.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/standard.png)
## Setting the industry standard with RDK-B
In 2014, Vantiva helped establish RDK-B with the donation of millions of lines of code, which enabled RDK to expand its applicability to broadband devices, setting a shared technical standard among suppliers. Now millions of home gateways across the planet use this software and RDK-B has become the industry standard software for cable modem and broadband devices — which is expanding to integrate other technologies, such as RDK-V.
## Embedded across Vantiva devices
Network service providers (NSPs) understand that ultra-broadband and gigabit services need more than just technical performance, they also require a high-quality end-user experience. RDK-B standardizes functionalities for broadband devices, enabling cable operators to efficiently deploy different services to a large customer base, making it possible to more easily manage different functions — including Wi-Fi and Multimedia over Coax Alliance (MoCA) and Internet of Things (IoT) controllers.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/group_speaking.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/world.png)
## A global success
Today, the RDK community comprises more than 600 companies worldwide, including customer premises equipment (CPE) manufacturers, SoC vendors, software developers, system integrators, and service providers. Over 30 video and service providers across North America, Europe, Latin America, and Asia are members of the RDK community across evaluation, testing, trials and deployment.
The number of RDK devices deployed worldwide continues to grow, currently surpassing 80 million across leading video and broadband service providers.
