**Software**
# PRPL
The prpl Foundation is an open-source, community-driven, collaborative non-profit organization dedicated to enhancing the security and interoperability of embedded devices.
**OVERVIEW**
## About PRPL
Prpl is a diverse community of service providers, OEMs, silicon vendors, ISVs, and open-source developers dedicated to creating standardized, carrier-grade customer premises equipment CPE through open-source software and open APIs.
[Click here to visit the PRPL Foundation website](https://prplfoundation.org/)
## Open-source  
**flexibility & control**
Rooted in open-source software like OpenWrt, prpl offers complete flexibility to developers and manufacturers, allowing them to fully customize the software to meet specific needs by adding or removing features without restrictions from larger ecosystems.
Prpl also helps manufacturers avoid vendor lock-in, enabling them to maintain full control over their device’s software environment.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/banner_text1.png)
## Optimized performance
Prpl enables the creation of highly optimized software tailored specifically to the hardware of CPE, resulting in better performance, especially in resource-constrained environments, by eliminating unnecessary layers of abstraction or services. With a focus on real-time processing, prpl-equipped set-top boxes can efficiently handle demanding tasks like video processing and complex networking functions.
## Interoperability **& Virtualization**
Prpl promotes open standards, enhancing interoperability with other devices and systems in the home network. This is crucial in environments where the gateways must communicate with devices like home automation systems. Prpl also supports virtualization, allowing multiple services to run on the same hardware without interference. This enables CPE to serve as multi-purpose devices such as media server or IoT hub without compromising performance or security.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/carre_terre.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/standard.png)
## Cost-effective development
Prpl’s open-source nature eliminates licensing fees, reducing costs for manufacturers, especially for lower-cost or mass-market devices. Without the need to comply with mandatory features or certification processes of proprietary systems, manufacturers can concentrate on the core functionality of their CPE, further reducing development and maintenance costs.
## Vantiva’s contribution to PRPL
As an active member of the prpl Foundation, Vantiva contributes to high-velocity, service-driven innovation on CPE by supporting the harmonization of interfaces in open APIs and delivering open-source reference implementations of common infrastructure.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/group_speaking.png)

**Software**
# Vantiva Homeware™
**OVERVIEW**
## Leveraging and extending  
**the power of openwrt**
Vantiva’s Homeware™ software solution leverages openWRT to deliver a scalable software stack for home gateways. An open-source software development kit (SDK) for service providers, Homeware provides a standard platform to build, deploy, and support new services more efficiently. We have extended openWRT to make it carrier-grade while maintaining the overall architecture — the result is an intuitive software solution that is open, apps-ready, interoperable, and secure.
## An open-source platform
We believe in the power of open-source software — the inherent collaboration leads to faster time-to-market and improved software quality. Vantiva Homeware benefits from a large community of developers who are continuously testing and contributing to the improvement of the platform. To ensure the ongoing growth and success of this, we also contribute back to the OpenWRT community to improve the open-source community’s projects.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/homeware.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/world.png)
## Seamless interoperability
Vantiva Homeware is built on the principle of strong, seamless interoperability — which has ensured successful deployment in more than 50 countries across various configurations. This compatibility greatly reduces time to market and gives service providers the freedom to choose.
## Designed for new applications
Homeware is an SDK for service providers to develop unique and fully customized applications on their gateways. This enables operators to generate new services and improve average revenue per user (ARPU) or optimize existing services and reduce total cost of ownership (TCO). Third-party developers can easily code compatible apps or choose from a catalog of pre-integrated innovative apps from Vantiva’s Advanced Technology Partner Program. One example is Homeware’s Life Cycle Management application, which improves broadband service availability by decoupling application upgrades and maintenance from the gateway core software.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/kid_on_phone.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/touchscreen_security.png)
## Three rigorous security checks
Vantiva’s Homeware is based on an overall software architecture with end-to-end security by design: from bootup to the installation of applications via lifecycle management. Software undergoes three rigorous security checks to reduce the risk of vulnerabilities: during development, during validation, and even once products are delivered. At regular intervals, the products are validated by independent third-party security labs.
## Improving security for customer premises equipment (CPE)
Protect home gateways, set-top box platforms, and end-users’ data with Vantiva’s advanced CPE security.
[ See more  ](https://connected.vantiva.com/en/white-paper/x-factor-fiber-strategy-v)

**Set-top boxes**
# TV & digital content that connects
Nothing creates lasting memories like an immersive entertainment experience with the people you love. We push the limits of set-top boxes, integrating the best in content, image, sound, and artificial intelligence technologies for a truly unforgettable experience.
  * [OVERVIEW](https://www.vantiva.com/connected-home/video-solutions/tv-digital-content-that-connects/#overview)

**OVERVIEW**
## The epicenter of entertainment
Set-top boxes have become the heart of our entertainment systems, seamlessly bridging traditional television and cutting-edge digital content. As the demand for personalized viewing experiences grows, these versatile devices are set to play an even more pivotal role in the future, leveraging AI and new emerging technologies to deliver innovative and immersive media solutions.
Benefits 
## Set-top boxes redefined

## Introducing Soundscape™: **a masterpiece in technology**

Innovative technology from Vantiva and our world-leading entertainment partners brings an immersive theater-like experience straight to viewers’ living rooms.
**BENEFITS**
## Phenomenal 3D sound with Dolby Atmos™
The ultimate Dolby Atmos set-top box, Soundscape creates true sound immersion, with a realistic 3D rendering of sound and precise localization of static or moving objects. The Dolby Atmos technology identifies individual audio objects and manages each one independently which — when combined with classic surround sound effects — creates more realism and better immersion. The HARMAN patented Slip Port Design takes this further, creating clear sound repetition on each side for a deeper 3D sound experience.

  * 2 Tweeters 20W

**Software**
# Navigate IQ™
NaviGate IQ™ is the single source of knowledge for marketing, technical operations, and quality assurance teams who want to make the best of their set-top boxes’ data.
**OVERVIEW**
## From rough data  
**to actionable knowledge**
The television landscape has evolved drastically over the last few years. There are more video services that can be offered on any network and on any platform. For Pay-TV Operators, the main challenge is providing subscribers with the right content at the right price. This requires a deep understanding of subscribers — how do they consume video content? What’s attractive to them? Which parts of the service are they not interested in? Vantiva NaviGate IQ™ helps Operators understand if their services are truly relevant, competitive, and engaging.
## Turn knowledge  
**into decision making**
Vantiva’s NaviGate IQ solution consists of a lightweight monitoring agent running on the subscriber’s set-top box (STB) leveraging Android TV™ APIs. These analytics allow a deeper understanding of the subscribers’ usage of Android TV applications and services on the STB, displayed as a convenient analytics dashboard.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/standard.png)
## Service usage analytics
Access a consolidated view of subscriber behavior with the TV service and the related environment through service usage analytics. This includes the number of devices, STB usage, use of features like voice control, details on the connected TV display, recording habits, and even account sharing information.
## Content usage analytics
Content usage analytics provide comprehensive information on both the video and applications preferred by subscribers. Understand the TV content and on-demand video a subscriber watches, which content providers they prefer, how much they’re watching, which applications they’re using (or removing), and what time they prefer to watch.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/ordi_analytics.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/comics.png)
## Quality of experience  
**and customer support analytics**
Today, subscribers require a consistent, reliable experience . Quality of Experience and Customer Support analytics enable operators to identify the technical performance and usage of the STB. These analytics provide information such as Wi-Fi® usage and strength, boot time, internet network loss, STB hardware and software details, security parameters, and more.
## Navigate IQ solution brief
Vantiva’s NaviGate IQ solution consists of a lightweight monitoring agent that resides on the subscriber’s set-top box and leverages Android TV APIs. Our comprehensive solution brief offers many actionable insights for operators to leverage customer data from their Android TV set-top boxes.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/navigateIQ_graph-1.png)
## Learn more  
**about Navigate IQ™**
One of Pay TV Operators’ primary challenges is delivering the right content mix at the right price — at Vantiva, we know this means deeply understanding subscribers’ context, video consumption habits, and preferences. Equally important is identifying which aspects of the service are not valued by subscribers.
Vantiva NaviGate IQ™ helps operators assess the relevance, competitiveness, and quality of their video services, ensuring subscribers’ needs are effectively met.
[ Download the solution description  ](https://connected.vantiva.com/en/solution-brief-navigate-iq-2023-v)

**Software**
# Android TV™:  
**a smart TV OS**
## Feature-rich  
**Android TV software**
Our innovative, feature-rich Vantiva Android TV software helps operators add value to the end user experience, from easy access to their favorite apps to essential features and robust security — we can help you deliver a seamless viewing experience to end users.
Designed for smart TVs and streaming devices, Android TV simplifies the way people access and interact with the content and entertainment they love on their TVs.
## Innovate with Android TV:  
**a path to better products**
Explore two key rules for developing Android TV set-top boxes, and how this compares to Linux-based products.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/standard.png)
## The industry leader  
**in Android TV software**
In the 10 years that Vantiva has been a Google premium partner, we have earned a reputation as the market leader in Android TV. We help operators provide a premium entertainment experience by offering support for applications — including development, integration, and certification — and a strategy of continuous innovation. Our firmware helps operators harness existing and emerging technologies, such as Wi-Fi® repeaters, data analytics, IoT, and far field voice to ensure that they stay in the center of their customer’s world.
## Android TV **operator tier**
We offer the Android TV Operator Tier program which enables greater customization for providers who want to create a stronger branded experience for their subscribers. Vantiva’s TV stack adds new depth to Android TV set-top box devices by seamlessly integrating traditional Pay-TV features into the Android TV environment, such as front-end configurations, security solutions, or parental control. Vantiva’s software approach also minimizes dependencies between the TV stack and partner apps, ensuring seamless integration with third-party software modules.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/settopbox.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/comics.png)
## Top Android TV certification
Vantiva is the industry-leader in software integration and certification for Android TV set-top box platforms. We have implemented more than 30 Android TV letter upgrades and the most Netflix, Amazon Prime Video, and Disney+ certifications in the industry. As a manufacturer, we are responsible for certifying the device for Android TV and providing ongoing maintenance. Fortunately, we have the most experienced dedicated test and certification teams in the industry, significantly reducing the time to market for operators.
## Android TV security
Content providers are strengthening their content-protection requirements, making Android TV Security an essential feature in the choice of their device manufacturer. Vantiva has more than 20 years of CAS (Conditional Access Systems) and DRM (Digital Rights Management) solutions integration experience, dedicated security teams, and ISO 27001 certification. We understand the security needs of Pay-TV operators, and work to ensure solid, secure content protection solutions in a fast-evolving market.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/touchscreen_security.png)

**Software**
# RDK-V lab  
accelerator
## The open-source  
**software platform**
Reference Design Kit for Video (RDK-V) is the open-source software platform that provides a broad range of video functionality to home gateways and set-top boxes (STBs). The Vantiva RDK-V Lab Accelerator is our way of contributing directly to this open-source platform, encouraging innovation with teams across the globe.
RDK-V accelerates the deployment of next-gen video products and services and simplifies the customization of the application and user interface.
## RDK-V, defined
RDK-V is part of the Reference Design Kit (RDK) platform, a fully modular, portable, customizable open-source platform used by hundreds of companies, including Vantiva. RDK-V enables developers and operators to use a unified software stack for STBs and home gateways across a broad range of complex video and management functions — rendering, content, content security, device management, networking, and more.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/rdk_image.png)
## Embedded across  
**Vantiva devices**
Vantiva offers a high level of integration of RDK-V in its different hardware platforms. Our RDK set-top boxes are deployed with Comcast and their syndication partners, which are also moving beyond the US market to reach European operators. Every RDK-V STB produced is validated with TDK and combined with our own additional end-to-end tests with operators’ infrastructures and streams.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/liste_produit1.png)
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/world.png)
## RDK-V teams  
**across the globe**
The RDK-V Lab Accelerator is truly an international project. Our teams based in Norcross, GA, Sunnyvale, CA, and Philadelphia, PA, support our US customers. The team in our R&C center in Rennes, France supports our EMEA customers and works on the hardware and software architecture, plus product and program management. Our teams in Chennai, India and Beijing, China work on the different building blocks, such as the loader, validation, and drivers. Together, they all ensure that Vantiva is supercharging innovation across the RDK-V platform.
## A founding contributor **to RDK**
Vantiva has been a committed innovator to RDK, donating millions of lines of code to support the platform. We believe in the power of RDK. As an independent, open-source solution, RDK is accessible to any operator and is developed and maintained by an active, engaged community of developers across the world. With tens of million devices in the world, Vantiva leads the market in North America and Europe. And with the RDK-V Lab Accelerator, Vantiva is helping RDK-V reach a new level of momentum.
![](https://www.vantiva.com/app/uploads/2024/08/group_speaking.png)

### **eBook**
# **AI for the home: a Service Provider guide to Enhancing Customer Satisfaction**
What if AI could revolutionize the way Service Providers operate while enhancing customer satisfaction in the most efficient way possible?
At Vantiva, we believe AI solutions should be brought closer to home. By exploring the potential of home edge AI for privacy-first applications and enhancing network edge processing for real-time use cases, we aim to drive innovation that is smarter, faster, and more secure.
Curious? Download our comprehensive guide,  _AI for the Home_ , to explore the potential of distributed AI architecture and how it can transform your business. Inside, you’ll find key insights into hierarchical AI, resource sharing with NPUs, and much more.

### **Case Study**
# **Pioneering Connectivity: Vantiva’s eSIM-Enabled 5G FWA Gateway**
Discover how Vantiva revolutionized broadband in the Middle East with the region’s first eSIM-enabled 5G Fixed Wireless Access (FWA) gateway. This cutting-edge solution addresses logistical challenges, enhances coverage by 40%, and boosts customer satisfaction through seamless self-installation and advanced network management tools. 
Learn about the innovative strategies, including bypassing traditional QR code setups and optimizing initial connectivity, that set new benchmarks for operational efficiency and user experience. Packed with insights on leveraging eSIM technology and its integration with Indoor5G™ and NaviGate Companion™, this case study unveils the future of connectivity.

### **Ebook**
### **Antenna Lab: Delivering optimal Wi-Fi experiences through in-house quality testing and design**
Wireless technology has become a mainstay of the modern home network. Consumer expectations around reliable, high-speed bandwidth and the ability to support many devices simultaneously without congestion or lag, anywhere in the home, all drive Service Provider demands for high-quality Wi-Fi® products. 
Antenna design, positioning, and isolation are crucial to the overall performance of a Wi-Fi device — and the root of many constraints during the engineering process. 
To discover how Vantiva deals with these challenges and the science behind our superior Wi-Fi performance, download our Ebook, "Antenna Lab: Delivering optimal Wi-Fi experiences through in-house quality testing and design”.

### **White paper**
# **The X-factors of a Successful Customer Premises Equipment Fiber Strategy**
Indeed, fiber networks bring unprecedented speed to the home via the main gateway. In fact, the ability to deliver Gigabit speeds to the home is becoming “normal”, with operators having more options in equipment selection and customers having more choices for delivery methods. The result is operators need to compete with differentiating features beyond speed.  
  
Read Vantiva's 2023 white paper that explains the most important factors - Interoperability, open software platforms, security, Wi-Fi performance, companion mobile app and sustainability - that empower the fiber gateway, making it robust, reliable, and future proof beyond speed. Vantiva thereby brings Peace of Mind to both the operator and the customer through these capabilities embedded in our Customer Premises Equipment (CPE) devices.
![Download x-factor Fiber strategy WP](https://connected.vantiva.com/hubfs/_VANTIVA%20DOWNLOAD%20PAGES/DOWNLOAD%202023%20Fiber.png)

### **Case Study**
# **Understanding Consumers Need, Delivering a Superior Entertainment Experience**
LG U+ Soundbar Black captures attention of Korean consumers and elevates the NSP's position as a provider of premium entertainment experiences.   
  
TV manufacturers have progressed over the years to create products that deliver an impressive image quality. But the thin design of a TV screen does not allow its integrated speakers to deliver great sound. As more and more quality content is distributed through their preferred OTT platforms, users become more and more dissatisfied with the lack of audio quality.  
  
Discover how LG U+ Soundbar Black, based on Vantiva Soundscape, a single high end Android TV 12 Set-Top-Box combined with a HARMAN with Sound-by-JBL audio solution, was designed precisely to address this customer unmet need. 
![Download Soundbar case study](https://connected.vantiva.com/hubfs/_VANTIVA%20DOWNLOAD%20PAGES/DOWNLOAD%202023%20Soundbar.png)

### **Solution description**
### **Transforming data into customer insight**
To meet the objective of providing the best possible offers to their customers, Pay TV Operators must understand how their subscribers consume video content and what is most important for them. Conversely, they also need to identify which part of the proposed service is not valuable for their subscribers. The Vantiva NaviGate IQ™ solution helps Pay TV operators understand the relevance, competitiveness, and value of their proposed video services.  
  
Explore the details of the Vantiva NaviGate IQ™ solution and the benefits for Pay TV operators and their subscribers.
![NaviGate IQ 2023](https://connected.vantiva.com/hubfs/NaviGate%20IQ%202023.png)
